Title: SUV smashes into Cape Coral toll booth
Author Name: Sarah Mankowitz
Excerpt: 
Publish Date: Updated: 7:44 PM EDT Mar 30, 2024
URL: https://www.abc-7.com/article/suv-smashes-into-cape-coral-toll-booth/60349726
Post Content:


					An SUV smashed into the Cape Coral Bridge toll booth plaza on Saturday.The SUV smashed into the poles and left debris everywhere.The Lee County Sheriff's Office confirms multiple agencies responded to the scene.The front of the SUV was crushed, and now pieces of the vehicle still surround the toll booth.People who live next to the plaza say they saw police in the area."Earlier today, my dog was going crazy, and there were sheriffs and EMS and firefighters all parked in our area, but I didn't hear anything; I just saw everyone, and I was kinda curious as to what was going on," said Esther Fernandez.Another resident recalled numerous accidents on the bridge but never quite like this."Frequently, there are accidents on the bridge, but never at the actual toll plaza," said Christar Damiano.Count on ABC7 as we work to find out what caused this crash. We have reached out to CCPD and are waiting for a response.

<div class="article-content--body-text-raw">
					An SUV smashed into the Cape Coral Bridge toll booth plaza on Saturday.The SUV smashed into the poles and left debris everywhere.The Lee County Sheriff's Office confirms multiple agencies responded to the scene.The front of the SUV was crushed, and now pieces of the vehicle still surround the toll booth.People who live next to the plaza say they saw police in the area."Earlier today, my dog was going crazy, and there were sheriffs and EMS and firefighters all parked in our area, but I didn't hear anything; I just saw everyone, and I was kinda curious as to what was going on," said Esther Fernandez.Another resident recalled numerous accidents on the bridge but never quite like this."Frequently, there are accidents on the bridge, but never at the actual toll plaza," said Christar Damiano.Count on ABC7 as we work to find out what caused this crash. We have reached out to CCPD and are waiting for a response.
				</div>

<div class="article-content--body-text">
<p>An SUV smashed into the Cape Coral Bridge toll booth plaza on Saturday.</p><p>The SUV smashed into the poles and left debris everywhere.</p><!-- article/blocks/side-floater -->
<div class="article-content--body-wrapper-side-floater">
<!-- blocks/ad.twig -->

<!-- blocks/ad.twig -->
</div>
<!-- article/blocks/side-floater --><p>The Lee County Sheriff's Office confirms multiple agencies responded to the scene.</p><p>The front of the SUV was crushed, and now pieces of the vehicle still surround the toll booth.</p><p>People who live next to the plaza say they saw police in the area.</p><p>"Earlier today, my dog was going crazy, and there were sheriffs and EMS and firefighters all parked in our area, but I didn't hear anything; I just saw everyone, and I was kinda curious as to what was going on," said Esther Fernandez.</p>
<p>Another resident recalled numerous accidents on the bridge but never quite like this.</p><div class="cream-inline hidden" id="cream-inline-rec">
</div>
<p>"Frequently, there are accidents on the bridge, but never at the actual toll plaza," said Christar Damiano.</p><p>Count on ABC7 as we work to find out what caused this crash. We have reached out to CCPD and are waiting for a response.</p>
</div>

				<div class="article-content--body-teaser">
					
				</div>

				<div class="article-content--body-text-raw">
					An SUV smashed into the Cape Coral Bridge toll booth plaza on Saturday.The SUV smashed into the poles and left debris everywhere.The Lee County Sheriff's Office confirms multiple agencies responded to the scene.The front of the SUV was crushed, and now pieces of the vehicle still surround the toll booth.People who live next to the plaza say they saw police in the area."Earlier today, my dog was going crazy, and there were sheriffs and EMS and firefighters all parked in our area, but I didn't hear anything; I just saw everyone, and I was kinda curious as to what was going on," said Esther Fernandez.Another resident recalled numerous accidents on the bridge but never quite like this."Frequently, there are accidents on the bridge, but never at the actual toll plaza," said Christar Damiano.Count on ABC7 as we work to find out what caused this crash. We have reached out to CCPD and are waiting for a response.
				</div>

				<div class="article-content--body-text">
																<p>An SUV smashed into the Cape Coral Bridge toll booth plaza on Saturday.</p><p>The SUV smashed into the poles and left debris everywhere.</p><!-- article/blocks/side-floater -->

<!-- article/blocks/side-floater --><p>The Lee County Sheriff's Office confirms multiple agencies responded to the scene.</p><p>The front of the SUV was crushed, and now pieces of the vehicle still surround the toll booth.</p><p>People who live next to the plaza say they saw police in the area.</p><p>"Earlier today, my dog was going crazy, and there were sheriffs and EMS and firefighters all parked in our area, but I didn't hear anything; I just saw everyone, and I was kinda curious as to what was going on," said Esther Fernandez.</p>


<p>Another resident recalled numerous accidents on the bridge but never quite like this.</p><div id="cream-inline-rec" class="cream-inline hidden">
</div>
<p>"Frequently, there are accidents on the bridge, but never at the actual toll plaza," said Christar Damiano.</p><p>Count on ABC7 as we work to find out what caused this crash. We have reached out to CCPD and are waiting for a response.</p>
